# q-fin.CP [[Back]](#toc)

### [195] [Volatility Calibration via Automatic Local Regression](https://arxiv.org/abs/2509.16334)
*Ruozhong Yang,Hao Qin,Charlie Che,Liming Feng*

Main category: q-fin.CP

TL;DR: 提出一种预校准平滑方法，通过局部回归去噪市场数据，显著改善局部波动率模型的表面平滑性和希腊值稳定性，同时保持对市场数据的高拟合精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 局部波动率模型校准本质上是不适定问题，导致波动率曲面尖锐、希腊值不稳定，影响 exotic derivatives 的对冲可靠性。

Method: 在LV校准前，采用局部回归方法对市场观测数据进行预处理，自动最小化渐近条件均方误差，生成去噪后的输入数据。

Result: 数值实验表明，该方法显著提升了LV曲面的平滑性，大幅改善了奇异期权希腊值的稳定性，且计算成本几乎无增加，同时保持了对市场价格的高精度拟合。

Conclusion: 预校准平滑方法能有效解决LV模型校准中的不适定性问题，提升定价与对冲的可靠性，可无缝集成到现有校准流程中。

Abstract: Managing exotic derivatives requires accurate mark-to-market pricing and
stable Greeks for reliable hedging. The Local Volatility (LV) model
distinguishes itself from other pricing models by its ability to match
observable market prices across all strikes and maturities with high accuracy.
However, LV calibration is fundamentally ill-posed: finite market observables
must determine a continuously-defined surface with infinite local volatility
parameters. This ill-posed nature often causes spiky LV surfaces that are
particularly problematic for finite-difference-based valuation, and induces
high-frequency oscillations in solutions, thus leading to unstable Greeks. To
address this challenge, we propose a pre-calibration smoothing method that can
be integrated seamlessly into any LV calibration workflow. Our method
pre-processes market observables using local regression that automatically
minimizes asymptotic conditional mean squared error to generate denoised inputs
for subsequent LV calibration. Numerical experiments demonstrate that the
proposed pre-calibration smoothing yields significantly smoother LV surfaces
and greatly improves Greek stability for exotic options with negligible
additional computational cost, while preserving the LV model's ability to fit
market observables with high fidelity.

</details>


### [196] [Analysis of the Impact of an Execution Algorithm with an Order Book Imbalance Strategy on a Financial Market Using an Agent-based Simulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2509.16912)
*Shuto Endo,Takanobu Mizuta,Isao Yagi*

Main category: q-fin.CP

TL;DR: 该研究通过多智能体模拟，在人工市场中构建并测试了一种考虑订单簿失衡（OBI）的交易执行算法，发现OBI在价格不稳定市场中能显著提升执行表现，对虚假挂单操纵具有鲁棒性，但在稳定市场中效果依赖于订单切片设计。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 由于现实中难以分离OBI对执行效果的影响，缺乏实证支持，因此需要通过可控的多智能体模拟环境来研究OBI在执行算法中的作用。

Method: 构建一个基于OBI的执行算法，并在多种人工市场情景（稳定、不稳定、存在虚假挂单）下，与传统忽略OBI的算法进行对比，通过多智能体模拟分析其性能和机制。

Result: （1）在稳定市场中，OBI策略的表现依赖于订单切片数量；（2）在价格波动市场中，OBI算法优于传统方法；（3）在虚假挂单操纵下，OBI策略未显著变差，显示其对操纵具有较强鲁棒性。

Conclusion: OBI是一个有用的执行信号，尤其在波动市场中可提升执行效果，且对操纵不敏感；但在稳定市场中，其效益受订单切片方式影响较大。

Abstract: Order book imbalance (OBI) - buy orders minus sell orders near the best quote
- measures supply-demand imbalance that can move prices. OBI is positively
correlated with returns, and some investors try to use it to improve
performance. Large orders placed at once can reveal intent, invite
front-running, raise volatility, and cause losses. Execution algorithms
therefore split parent orders into smaller lots to limit price distortion. In
principle, using OBI inside such algorithms could improve execution, but prior
evidence is scarce because isolating OBI's effect in real markets is nearly
impossible amid many external factors.
  Multi-agent simulation offers a way to study this. In an artificial market,
individual actors are agents whose rules and interactions form the model. This
study builds an execution algorithm that accounts for OBI, tests it across
several market patterns in artificial markets, and analyzes mechanisms,
comparing it with a conventional (OBI-agnostic) algorithm.
  Results: (i) In stable markets, the OBI strategy's performance depends on the
number of order slices; outcomes vary with how the parent order is partitioned.
(ii) In markets with unstable prices, the OBI-based algorithm outperforms the
conventional approach. (iii) Under spoofing manipulation, the OBI strategy is
not significantly worse than the conventional algorithm, indicating limited
vulnerability to spoofing.
  Overall, OBI provides a useful signal for execution. Incorporating OBI can
add value - especially in volatile conditions - while remaining reasonably
robust to spoofing; in calm markets, benefits are sensitive to slicing design.

</details>


### [197] [FinFlowRL: An Imitation-Reinforcement Learning Framework for Adaptive Stochastic Control in Finance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2509.17964)
*Yang Li,Zhi Chen,Steve Y. Yang,Ruixun Zhang*

Main category: q-fin.CP

TL;DR: FinFlowRL 是一个结合了模仿学习和强化学习的金融随机控制新框架，通过在噪声空间中微调预训练的元策略，并采用动作分块方法，在多变市场条件下表现优于传统方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统随机控制方法依赖简化假设，在现实市场中表现不佳，尤其在市场条件变化时性能下降。

Method: 结合模仿学习和强化学习，首先通过多个专家策略预训练自适应元策略，然后在噪声空间中通过强化学习进行微调，并采用动作分块生成动作序列以应对金融市场的非马尔可夫性。

Result: FinFlowRL 在多种市场条件下始终优于单独优化的专家策略。

Conclusion: FinFlowRL 能有效提升金融随机控制在复杂和动态市场环境中的鲁棒性和性能。

Abstract: Traditional stochastic control methods in finance rely on simplifying
assumptions that often fail in real world markets. While these methods work
well in specific, well defined scenarios, they underperform when market
conditions change. We introduce FinFlowRL, a novel framework for financial
stochastic control that combines imitation learning with reinforcement
learning. The framework first pretrains an adaptive meta policy by learning
from multiple expert strategies, then finetunes it through reinforcement
learning in the noise space to optimize the generation process. By employing
action chunking, that is generating sequences of actions rather than single
decisions, it addresses the non Markovian nature of financial markets.
FinFlowRL consistently outperforms individually optimized experts across
diverse market conditions.

</details>

# physics.data-an [[Back]](#toc)

### [198] [Comment on Frank Porter, "Confidence intervals for the Poisson distribution"](https://arxiv.org/abs/2509.17339)
*Robert D. Cousins*

Main category: physics.data-an

TL;DR: 本文讨论了Porter对泊松分布置信区间的研究评论，指出其在似然函数存在性问题上的观点与Feldman和作者（FC）存在根本分歧，并重点分析了该分歧及其影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 澄清Porter论文中关于似然比检验置信区间的误解，特别是关于参数空间中统计模型不存在区域的似然函数是否存在这一根本问题。

Method: 通过理论分析和逻辑推理，比较Porter与Feldman-Cousins（FC）在似然函数存在性上的观点，并探讨其对置信区间构建的影响。

Result: 作者认为Porter的观点存在缺陷，强调在统计模型未定义的参数区域中似然函数不应存在，这对置信区间的构造具有重要影响。

Conclusion: 在构建置信区间时，应坚持似然函数仅在统计模型有效区域内定义的原则，FC方法在此基础上是合理的，而Porter的相关讨论需修正。

Abstract: Frank Porter has recently posted a review of "Confidence intervals for the
Poisson distribution" (arXiv:2509.02852). The long, diverse history of such
intervals is closely related to that of confidence intervals for the parameter
of the binomial distribution. While much of Porter's paper is enlightening and
food for thought, I believe that his discussion of the intervals advocated by
Gary Feldman and myself (FC) based on the likelihood ratio test
(arXiv:physics/9711021) is flawed. The fundamental point of disagreement is
whether or not the likelihood function exists in a part of parameter space
where the statistical model does not exist. (The new paper says yes; FC say
no.) Here, I focus mainly on that issue and the consequences, along with a few
other remarks.

</details>


### [199] [Particle Identification with MLPs and PINNs Using HADES Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2509.17685)
*Marvin Kohls*

Main category: physics.data-an

TL;DR: 提出一种应用于HADES数据的粒子鉴别方法，显著提升了稀有事件识别的效率和准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在核与粒子物理实验中，高纯度稀有事件样本的提取依赖于粒子识别的效率和准确性。

Method: 采用物理信息神经网络对完全重建的粒子轨迹候选者进行粒子识别。

Result: 相比传统方法，该方法显著提升了粒子识别性能。

Conclusion: 物理信息神经网络有望成为未来数据分析中的有力工具。

Abstract: In experimental nuclear and particle physics, the extraction of high-purity
samples of rare events critically depends on the efficiency and accuracy of
particle identification (PID). In this work, we present a PID method applied to
HADES data at the level of fully reconstructed particle track candidates. The
results demonstrate a significant improvement in PID performance compared to
conventional techniques, highlighting the potential of physics-informed neural
networks as a powerful tool for future data analyses.

</details>
